import { indianTranslations } from './indian';
import { europeanLanguages } from './european';
import { eastAsianLanguages } from './east-asian';
import { otherLanguages } from './other';
import { majorLanguages } from './major-languages';

// Language type definition - only languages with working translations
export type LanguageCode =
  | 'hi' | 'bn' | 'ta' | 'te' | 'mr' | 'gu' | 'pa' | 'kn' | 'ml' | 'or' | 'as' | 'ur' // Indian languages
  | 'es' | 'fr' | 'de' | 'it' | 'ru' | 'pt' | 'nl' | 'pl' | 'tr' | 'vi' // European & Major languages
  | 'zh' | 'ja' | 'ko' // East Asian languages
  | 'ar' | 'th'; // Other languages

// Consolidated translations object  
export const translations: Record<string, Record<string, string>> = {
  // Indian Languages (Fixed with dotted keys)
  ...indianTranslations,
  
  // European Languages
  ...europeanLanguages,
  
  // East Asian Languages
  ...eastAsianLanguages,
  
  // Other Languages
  ...otherLanguages,
  
  // Major World Languages
  ...majorLanguages,
};

// Export language categories for easier management
export const languageCategories = {
  indian: Object.keys(indianTranslations),
  european: Object.keys(europeanLanguages),
  eastAsian: Object.keys(eastAsianLanguages),
  other: Object.keys(otherLanguages),
  major: Object.keys(majorLanguages),
};

// Helper function to get all supported languages
export const getSupportedLanguages = (): LanguageCode[] => {
  return Object.keys(translations) as LanguageCode[];
};

// Helper function to check if a language is supported
export const isLanguageSupported = (lang: string): lang is LanguageCode => {
  return lang in translations;
};


import { translations } from './translations/index';

interface TranslationCache {
  [language: string]: {
    [key: string]: string;
  };
}

class TranslationService {
  private cache: TranslationCache = {};

  constructor() {
    this.loadFromLocalStorage();
  }

  private loadFromLocalStorage() {
    try {
      const cachedData = localStorage.getItem('ui_translation_cache');
      if (cachedData) {
        this.cache = JSON.parse(cachedData);
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.warn('Failed to load UI translation cache:', error);
    }
  }

  private saveToLocalStorage() {
    try {
      localStorage.setItem('ui_translation_cache', JSON.stringify(this.cache));
    } catch (error) {
      console.warn('Failed to save UI translation cache:', error);
    }
  }
  
  async translate(key: string, targetLanguage: string): Promise<string> {
    // Return original key for English
    if (targetLanguage === 'en') {
      return key;
    }

    // Check cache first
    if (this.cache[targetLanguage] && this.cache[targetLanguage][key]) {
      return this.cache[targetLanguage][key];
    }

    // Use static translation
    const langTranslations = translations[targetLanguage];
    const translatedText = (langTranslations && langTranslations[key]) ? langTranslations[key] : key;
    
    // Cache the result
    if (!this.cache[targetLanguage]) {
      this.cache[targetLanguage] = {};
    }
    this.cache[targetLanguage][key] = translatedText;
    this.saveToLocalStorage();

    return translatedText;
  }

  clearCache(language?: string): void {
    if (language) {
      delete this.cache[language];
    } else {
      this.cache = {};
    }
    this.saveToLocalStorage();
  }
}

export const translationService = new TranslationService();
